<p>My dear, I’m sure he meant to pay us back eventually. He’s a decent man.</p>
<p>The mother mouth-entity looks at DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE for a second, then flits away.</p>
<h1 id="toc312"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>Hmm?</p>
<p>The mother mouth-entity does not speak. The FATHER-ENTITY does.</p>
<h1 id="toc313"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>Ough. Yeah, being stiffed by a client has got to be the worst. I don’t care much for discussing work, but I’m sure I can spare some moments on the phone should you need it.</p>
<p>The FATHER-ENTITY nods.</p>
<p>The mother mouth-entity speaks, and the FATHER-ENTITY goes to speak over her. Rather than stop, she escalates. A small spat of screeches occurs, their plates clinking as they gesture a kind of violence. It’s resolved by a blow.</p>
<h1 id="toc314"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>Hey, hey! I’m sure it’s not <em>that</em> bad! You can always settle this in the house, right?</p>
<p>The mother mouth-entity rapidly clicks. She pulls away from the father, but does not stand. She looks around, examining the room, and with a deft motion, the FATHER-ENTITY takes something into his hand. It goes under the table.</p>
<p>The mother mouth-entity recoils for a second and genuinely screams, its eye fixed on where the father’s hand might be. Then she relaxes, adopting a posture almost as docile as DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE’s.</p>
<p>Her eye does not flit nor focus anymore.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE wipes its mouth and discards its trash. It sips on a chalice of wine, setting it down after each sip. The light glistens off its gold-plated exterior.</p>
<h1 id="toc315"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>Alright. Glad to see you two have settled. Now, I’m sure that, as you know, I’m due to retire soon.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE’s wife excitedly springs up, and chirps quickly with the FATHER-ENTITY. He responds, cutting her off after a few seconds.</p>
<h1 id="toc316"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>Yeah, wasn’t done yet. Anyways, I say this because I’d like to seek your advice: What do <em>you</em> think is a good way to use my time afterwards? I’ve thought quite a bit about it, I must admit, and I’ve not come up with much.”</p>
<p>The FATHER-ENTITY screeches for a solid minute. DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE nods several times throughout, occasionally prompting him on with a “Yes, I know.”</p>
<h1 id="toc317"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>Huh. I’d never thought of it like that. Thank you—see honey, I told you your FATHER-ENTITY was a decent man! May have drunk a bit, but I knew he could fix himself.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE and the FATHER-ENTITY nod and shake hand-tongues at this.</p>
<h1 id="toc318"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>I hope your retirement goes well, good sir.</p>
<p>They continue to discuss as the lights dim, the mother-entity docile and the WIFE-ENTITY shaking, as the curtain drops.</p>
<h4 id="toc319"><span>END SCENE.</span></h4>
</div>

<div class="script">
<h3 id="toc320"><span>ACT THREE, SCENE TWO</span></h3>
<hr/>
<p><span style="font-size:smaller;">800 words.</span><br/>
EXT. COURTYARD. LIGHT OUT.</p>
<p>There is a fountain at center-stage which casts a shadow on the crowd below, the only shadow in this STAGE drenched with light. They stand on unpaved ground, where large weeds bloom and the catgrasses bundle up in plumes. The weeds expose spikes that attract a large amount of worms and flies. No one winces at their bites and scratches, though they’re plentiful.</p>
<p>They are in the plaza of a larger building surrounding them. It's built in the traditional Indo-Islamic style, with tiny domes and thick walls. The windows are colored nigh-randomly, with lime-green being the only obvious motif.</p>
<p>The sun is navy-blue, and its light dilutes to the hue of a chlorinated pool as it travels through the air. A crowd of MOUTH-ENTITIES gather under it. They all gaze upwards, holding out their tongues in a salute.</p>
<p>In a balcony which juts out from the building, a black-robed PRIEST-ENTITY yells. It’s hunched forward, and claws at the air vaguely and reverently as its voice booms through the space. It exhibits glossolalia. And though the voice is amplified and strong, it is drenched in echo, and the words slip away into incoherence. The sound is too distant.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE tries to pray. It prostrates itself, but cannot remain on the ground, and it rises every few seconds to keep from being trampled. Its face is scrunched, its distress obvious.</p>
<p>Its WIFE-ENTITY pats it on the shoulder and joins the crowd in their worship. DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE squints to hear her.</p>
<h1 id="toc321"><span>WIFE-ENTITY</span></h1>
<p>This will not be how it is forever.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE trembles under the tone of the ocean of people; <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">his</span> <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">wife</span> stays at his side, simply quiet.</p>
<h1 id="toc322"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc323"><span>(MEEKLY)</span></h1>
<p>I know. I know I should be better at this.</p>
<p>The WIFE-ENTITY clicks at it, giving some reassurance better left unheard. DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE sighs and kneels on the ground, looking as straight upwards as possible.</p>
<h1 id="toc324"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc325"><span>(Steadily)</span></h1>
<p>Glory be to the Savior. Glory be to the Savior. Glory be to the Savior…</p>
<p>While DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE repeats the maxim, the PRIEST-ENTITY holds out its appendages, letting the viscera drip down onto the crowd. They roar. Their tongues flow towards it, and they walk to the stuff with adoration. Some join the glossolalia, letting their tongues violently shake as they speak. Others jump in the air and spit on the ground.</p>
<p>Most of them chant.</p>
<h1 id="toc326"><span>MOUTH-ENTITIES</span></h1>
<p>PRAISE FOR THE ONE ABOVE US WHO BRINGS DOWN IN WISDOM THAT WHAT WILL SAVE US, THAT WHAT BRINGS US PEACE, THAT WHAT GLUES US TOGETHER. MAKE US AS A JAR, JOIN US WITH THE POTTER'S WHEEL AS WE JOIN YOU WITH OUR TONGUES AND SOUL.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE’s chant becomes quieter, his eyes screw shut, and the WIFE-ENTITY crouches to his level.</p>
<h1 id="toc327"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc328"><span>(Rapidly)</span></h1>
<p>Glory beta’th saviour glory be to d’savior glory’b to the savior…</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE stops as its speech becomes incoherent. It screeches in frustration, and it pounds the ground once, rising to its feet and holding the WIFE-ENTITY near. Some mixture of self-abasement and fear lies in its eyes.</p>
<h1 id="toc329"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>How do you do it, love? How do you <em>feel</em> the Savior entering? I've tried for so <em>fucking</em> long, and he runs from me in the visions! He runs!</p>
<p>The WIFE-ENTITY holds it. Both rock to an invisible cadence for a bit, and it takes an accidental hit from a fellow churchgoer for them to separate.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-8" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-8')">8</a></sup></p>
<p>She speaks as they move to the corner, away from the screaming and splattering.</p>
<h1 id="toc330"><span>WIFE-ENTITY</span></h1>
<p>You must try harder, love. You can always try harder.</p>
<h1 id="toc331"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>How do you <em>try</em> with love! How can you summon love? How can you make something in you that should be there! The people around me, they <em>love</em> and they don't need to <em>know</em>. I <em>need</em> to be like them! How else do you think I'll be in his favor, if I can't even manage to put him in mine?</p>
<p>She comes to his side, understanding his true worry.</p>
<p>The crowd almost drowns them out, but through some memetic miracle, they remain perfectly understandable, and not a word is lost.</p>
<h1 id="toc332"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>So what then?</p>
<p>The WIFE-ENTITY approaches. It does not resist, and it begins shaking as she embraces it.</p>
<h1 id="toc333"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>I didn't earn you.</p>
<p>The WIFE-ENTITY coos.</p>
<h1 id="toc334"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>You know that doesn't matter. I wasted myself in here. I <em>deprived</em> him. And I did it of my own volition. I can't…</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE faces towards the audience and falls — <em>collapses</em> — to its knees.</p>
<h1 id="toc335"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc336"><span>(Tearfully)</span></h1>
<p>I don't even remember your name.<br/>
Forgive me.<br/>
I can never stop asking forgiveness.</p>
<p>The WIFE-ENTITY touches it on the shoulders, massaging it.</p>
<p>Suddenly, <strong>he</strong> springs up from the ground — forcefully, passionately.</p>
<h1 id="toc337"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc338"><span>(With determination)</span></h1>
<p>I can't stay here.</p>
<h1 id="toc339"><span>WIFE-ENTITY</span></h1>
<p>Love, where do you go?</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE navigates through the crowd. The light darkens as <strong>he</strong> exits stage left.</p>
<h4 id="toc340"><span>END SCENE.</span></h4>
</div>

<div class="script">
<h3 id="toc341"><span>ACT THREE, SCENE THREE.</span></h3>
<hr/>
<p><span style="font-size:smaller;">800 words.</span><br/>
INT. OFFICE. - DUSK.</p>
<p>A blank banner stretches over the top of DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE's cubicle. Ten mouth-entities accompany it. DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE smiles; one of the mouth-entities brought a cake for DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE, something to eat until they’re all full.</p>
<p><em>He</em> returns.</p>
<h1 id="toc342"><span>PARTNER</span></h1>
<p>Doubleplusnegfeel to look at DISPOSABLE exit, yes?</p>
<p>A couple of the MOUTH-ENTITIES nod.</p>
<h1 id="toc343"><span>PARTNER (CONT’D)</span></h1>
<p>Person: Yeswise, I am negfeel, yet triumph. Triumph to look at DISPOSABLE changes.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE sighs and massages its face for a moment, expressing exhaustion.</p>
<h1 id="toc344"><span>DISPOSABLLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>You’re right. Damn right, PARTNER.</p>
<p>The PARTNER grins and flips a coin.</p>
<h1 id="toc345"><span>PARTNER</span></h1>
<p>Heads. Always heads.</p>
<h1 id="toc346"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc347"><span>(CONTEMPTUOSLY)</span></h1>
<p>Yes, I’m sure it will always go well for you.</p>
<p>The PARTNER continues flipping his coin as DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE turns to face the rest of the MOUTH-ENTITIES. It coughs.</p>
<h3 id="toc348"><span>THE STORY WILL PRESENTLY CONTINUE.</span></h3>
<h1 id="toc349"><span>MOUTH-ENTITY</span></h1>
<p>IT IS NOW GREAT TO EAT OFFERING! ASSUREDLY, THIS IS THE END, AND IT IS BEST TO LEARN NOW WHAT IT TASTES LIKE.</p>
<p>Everyone grabs glass plates from their pockets, folding them out with great ease, and they portion out the cake<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-9" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-9')">9</a></sup>.</p>
<h1 id="toc350"><span>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE</span></h1>
<p>I'm glad I was of use to the company, I tell you what.</p>
<p>The earpiece is static, but it clears out now. A chair creaks, and someone stands up.</p>
<h1 id="toc351"><span>COMMANDER</span></h1>
<p>I thought you were quite pretty as a little boy. Very pretty.</p>
<p>She waits a moment, and <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">he</span> does not respond. She chuckles, and the sound of ruffling cloth is heard. Her voice quivers.</p>
<h1 id="toc352"><span>COMMANDER (CONT'D)</span></h1>
<p>It hurt me that you did this to yourself. You hurt yourself, and you hurt me in the process. But I suppose you weren't meant to be in reality with me.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE finishes its cake first, and they awkwardly stand around, <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">his</span> thumbs in its pockets and the plate ready to be thrown away. It finds a trash can and walks to it slowly.</p>
<p>The mouth-entities engage in conversation around DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE. DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE listens in. The high-pitched warbling is more lucid than normal.</p>
<h1 id="toc353"><span>MOUTH-ENTITIES</span></h1>
<p>THE PROFITS FOR THIS QUARTER HAS TO GONE UP OVER TWENTY PERCENT PRAISE BE TO EXALTED FOR THIS VICTORY OVER U ALSO REMEMBER THAT YOU NEVER REALLY LEAVE—NO, YOU DON’T<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-10" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-10')">10</a></sup>—NOT WITH THE WRIGGLING INSIDE OF YOU THAT SOMEHOW YOU DID SOMETHING TO YOURSELF, UNDONABLE IT CANNOT BE; WE HOPE THAT YOU HAVE A GOOD LIFE OUTSIDE OF HERE, FELLOW, AND THAT YOU THINK IT WAS WORTH IT.</p>
<p>She sips from a drink and sighs. She stutters and hesitates, uncertain.</p>
<h1 id="toc354"><span>COMMANDER</span></h1>
<p>My… l-love, I, uhm, I hope you’re hap-py out there.</p>
<p>The COMMANDER pauses for a moment.</p>
<h1 id="toc355"><span>COMMANDER (CONT'D)</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc356"><span>(Contemplative)</span></h1>
<p>Uhm… what else…</p>
<h1 id="toc357"><span>COMMANDER (CONT’D)</span></h1>
<p>Please, no, I… stay! I know I had something.</p>
<h1 id="toc358"><span>COMMANDER (CONT’D)</span></h1>
<p>I… forgot. I suppose it wasn’t important, was it?</p>
<p>The COMMANDER disconnects her link to the earpiece.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE takes out the earpiece and throws it away with the roaches—they were never really its favorite, you know?—and cheers come now from the whole office, one-tone and clipped.</p>
<h1 id="toc359"><span>COWORKERS</span></h1>
<p>HURRAY!</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE is grateful and walks eyes closed, smiling. At least <em>they</em> are grateful and comprehending.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE exits stage back. The backboard is canCollide: false. HOUSE-LIGHT value: 0.</p>
<h3 id="toc360"><span>ABSTRACTIONS UNGOOD.</span></h3>

<p>The HOUSE LIGHTS return as DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE is driving down a wide stroad. It occupies the whole of the stage. The stage has expanded for it. It is cracked, weathered, 8 lanes wide, with no crossing or sidewalk. Occasionally, a big-box store connects to it, and they are the only variance in the endless, hopeless plain of red and yellowish dust.</p>
<h3 id="toc361"><span>WHITE NOISE WANTS TO BREAK THROUGH</span></h3>
<p>The BMW that DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE drives is falling apart with glee, but he does not react to this. The <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">BOAT</span> has left, and the power goes with it.</p>
<p>The car does not stop working as the alternator falls from its bottom, then the oil gasket, which pours an infinite amount of oil down the road. Soon, it is completely gone, the metal bones strewn throughout the road.</p>
<p>DISPOSABLE-ONE-TWELVE does not drive on or in anything anymore. For the first time in years, he looks around while his momentum carries him across the asphalt. He panics as he realizes the degree of freedom which he now enjoys.</p>
<p>The sun is white. It hammers down on him the way a mother suffocates with love a newborn child. It wants him to approach, and <em>the audience</em> can hear that from the speaker behind them, breathing heavily down their necks, observing them for its nexus.</p>
<p>The sun and the blackened moon fight for control of the sky, and the light levels on the <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">stage</span> begin to fluctuate rapidly. <em>Everything</em> is fluctuating rapidly, even YOU, and speed is building up as the <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">STAGE</span> stage falls down to the floor of reality, a foundation thirstily nearing. We are all knocked off our bearings.</p>
<p>Before we penetrate the barrier, JAKE manifests a blank business card.</p>
<h4 id="toc362"><span>END SCENE.</span></h4>
</div>

<div class="script">
<h3 id="toc363"><span>ACT THREE, SCENE FOUR.</span></h3>
<hr/>
<p><span style="font-size:smaller;">1000 words.</span><br/>
EXT. EXT.</p>
<p>JAKE is <a href="https://scp-wiki.wikidot.com/scp-3555" target="_blank">stretching</a> towards you from across the stars, across the sand, and across the stage, his waist shrinking into nothing. His shoulder flare out and he is <a href="https://youtu.be/vfCMtaNiMDM?t=45" target="_blank">powerful like a miter saw, like an industrial polymer presser.</a></p>
<p>Under the covers, with the buzzing in YOUR head increasing and the static stationary, JAKE begins to spin, and he touches YOU.</p>
<h1 id="toc364"><span>JAKE</span></h1>
<p>No.</p>
<p>He is unbig, anteLIGHTS and dancing happywise while downmoveing into strong wood. He bounds off the walls of the theater—his form strikes into the audience; none are harmed. He is a little wider than a centimeter, and he is a kilometer long, enough to scrape the stars. He is relieved;<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=t_jYOubJmfM" target="_blank">at last, he has achieved a dream</a>. The heat of plasma and blood comes down, splattering upon YOU.</p>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Complex_projective_space" target="_blank">A tear in his understanding of reality</a> pens before him as he centers himself. He makes a grab for it, a gambit uncertain in its outcome, for if he fails-</p>
<p>-he succeeds!—<br/>
<a href="https://scp-wiki.wikidot.com/scp-3380" target="_blank">Though he is now unclean</a>.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-11" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-11')">11</a></sup><br/>
The consequences will become shortly apparent, the wretching and the TV static all-consuming.<br/>
JAKE: I need you.<br/>
YOU are lifted from your seat.</p>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lambda-CDM_model#Overview" target="_blank">The page within which you worked turns</a>, making a wisp of sound near your ear, and you intersect with</p>
<h2 id="toc365"><span>the line.</span></h2>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tesseract#/media/File:8-cell-simple.gif" target="_blank">The intersection is an unholy marriage.</a><br/>
Death is certain to come for this, the cost of…<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-12" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-12')">12</a></sup></p>

<br/>
YOU survive. Aptly, it is <a href="https://scp-wiki.wikidot.com/scp-2682" target="_blank">Miracles from God.</a>
<p>In the untrespassable space, a choir sings, their harmonization and oblation even viewable to the deaf ear.</p>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proof_of_Heaven" target="_blank">There is a plane of mud there</a>, and the people in it are dirty and nasty things—definitionally. Pigs step carefully, trying to keep themselves clean. The globules bust—for some—and they fall in. Those ones do not stop falling. And the ones left must keep walking.</p>
<p>In another plane, <a href="https://forum.agoraroad.com/index.php?threads/dead-internet-theory-most-of-the-internet-is-fake.3011/" target="_blank">you find glass. Animals graze upon it, their faces distorted in it.</a> They are not conventionally alive. That is obvious. YOU cannot determine what makes them dead.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-13" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-13')">13</a></sup> The sun is white and strikes their skin, refracting light through mist. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ice-nine" target="_blank">A rainbow does not form in this place.</a></p>
<h3 id="toc366"><span>You must leave.</span></h3>
<h3 id="toc367"><span>You must leave.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-14" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-14')">14</a></sup></span></h3>

<br/>
You are filled with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clock_of_the_Long_Now" target="_blank">the glories of the Lord</a> present as you leave the manifold, its surface beginning to scratch at you. A thunderbolt strikes, but it cannot conduct itself in this place (your safety is guaranteed!) At the last possible moment, JAKE aids you.
<h3 id="toc368"><span>He absorbs the penance dealt for his hubris, the menacing force which sponsors him remaining unhurt.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-15" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-15')">15</a></sup></span></h3>
<p>By the power which is vested in him, the difficulties of life unlived will be distributed;</p>
<h1 id="toc369"><span>He shall save you from the trouble of it.</span></h1>
<p>JAKE: <a href="https://youtu.be/F7DebV5WN3Q?t=1272" target="_blank">Audacious. Do you think you can get away from this? I tell you now, better it is to drown hung by a millstone than to remain ignorant now.</a></p>
<h3 id="toc370"><span>But <em>God</em> damn you if you think that shedding stupidity is enough.</span></h3>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<p>From the west, a car approaches, a family tokenized by the bastard proselytizing angered. He’s stammering as they’re arriving, and they pass him by, their progress made.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-16" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-16')">16</a></sup></p>
</div>
<p>JAKE: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_King#Car_accident_and_aftermath" target="_blank">He</a> was broken in 6 places when the man hit him. It’s funny now, isn’t it? That’s good, that’s <a href="https://scp-wiki.wikidot.com/scp-2293" target="_blank">progress.</a><sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-17" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-17')">17</a></sup></p>
<h1 id="toc371"><span>JAKE: Why do you fear all of this? It’s not outside your understanding—on the contrary, it is quite easy for you. I think you're like me, and that is okay! All it means is that when you look at it, you know it instantly. <a href="https://www2.psych.ubc.ca/~henrich/pdfs/WeirdPeople.pdf" target="_blank">Be grateful.</a></span></h1>
<h1 id="toc372"><span>JAKE:</span></h1>
<p>And when you leave me tonight, leave me the knowledge I tried to make a change. Do not look at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_2.0#Web_1.0" target="_blank">neon</a>, but rather at eye's light.</p>
<p>The HOUSE-LIGHTS activate, blasting to void artificial panes of nullvalue light. The HOUSE-LIGHTS shine blue, and he spins, contracts, faster, the plaster with which he builds his attempts at laughing drying. He spins at a great, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zippe-type_centrifuge" target="_blank">rich</a> speed now. He heaves, his bowels shifting to make way for his gift to the world.</p>
<p>Somewhere, from a trigger unseen,<br/>
<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ia9R7T5eiTo" target="_blank">that choir begins to shift tongues</a>. The director falls to the floor, seizing. He is not strong enough to withstand the force which bears down upon him, sincerity writ large a raw, uncompromising, lividly lethal thing.<sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-18" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-18')">18</a></sup></p>
<p>Jake really fears.</p>
<p>Somewhere, a star thinks about fighting, rebelling, dancing. It</p>
<h1 id="toc373"><span>tries to get ten thousand of its family to join. They haven't time—haven’t you been busy too?</span></h1>
<h1 id="toc374"><span>Somewhere, <a href="https://archive.org/details/los-voceros-de-cristo-recuerdos-i/Escogido+Fui+de+Dios+-+Los+Voceros+de+Cristo.mp3" target="_blank">a tanned child grabs their headphones</a>, and he steps outside of his home at 12:53AM. The wife-entity commands him inside. For a moment, the star’s thought speaks to him.</span></h1>
<p><span style="text-decoration: line-through;">Mom: “Where are we? What've we done with our lives?”</span></p>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Supertask#Motion" target="_blank">No one comes.</a><sup class="footnoteref"><a class="footnoteref" href="javascript:;" id="footnoteref-19" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.utils.scrollToReference('footnote-19')">19</a></sup></p>
<p>In the gray theater, the black sphere drops, and an actor with the radiance of noonday snow emerges.<br/>
They</p>
<div style="text-align: right;">
<p>align</p>
</div>
<br/>
themselves, and the line vanishes, banished and protected within a broom closet. Damnation was inevitable.
<p><em><span style="color: #fcca03">On the Foundation, we are Secure.</span></em></p>
